## Decorator Node Mapping

### Class-level Decorator
- **Path**: `Program.body[0].declaration.decorators[0]`
- **Type**: `Decorator` → `CallExpression`
- **Pattern**: `@Controller('orders')`
- **Callee**: `Identifier` with name `"Controller"`
- **Arguments**: Single `Literal` with value `"orders"`

### Method-level Decorators
- **Path**: `Program.body[0].declaration.body.body[0].decorators`
- **Count**: 2 decorators
  1. `@Get(':id')` - `Decorator` → `CallExpression` with `Identifier("Get")` + `Literal(":id")`
  2. `@UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)` - `Decorator` → `CallExpression` with `Identifier("UseGuards")` + `Identifier("JwtAuthGuard")`

### Parameter Decorators (3 total)
All at path: `Program.body[0].declaration.body.body[0].value.params[n].decorators[0]`

1. **`@Param('id')`** (params[0])
   - Type: `Decorator` → `CallExpression`
   - Callee: `Identifier("Param")`
   - Arguments: `Literal("id")`
   - Attached to: `Identifier("id")` with `TSTypeAnnotation(TSStringKeyword)`

2. **`@CurrentUser()`** (params[1])
   - Type: `Decorator` → `CallExpression`
   - Callee: `Identifier("CurrentUser")`
   - Arguments: `[]` (empty array)
   - Attached to: `Identifier("user")` with `TSTypeAnnotation(TSTypeReference("UserEntity"))`

3. **`@Query('include')`** (params[2])
   - Type: `Decorator` → `CallExpression`
   - Callee: `Identifier("Query")`
   - Arguments: `Literal("include")`
   - Attached to: `Identifier("include")` with `TSTypeAnnotation(TSStringKeyword)`

## Key Observations for Visitor Patterns

### To match class decorators:
```typescript
"ClassDeclaration > Decorator > CallExpression[callee.name='Controller']"
```
**Matches**: Class-level `@Controller` decorators  
**Does NOT match**: Method decorators, parameter decorators, or non-Controller class decorators

### To match HTTP method decorators:
```typescript
"MethodDefinition > Decorator > CallExpression[callee.name=/^(Get|Post|Put|Delete|Patch)$/]"
```
**Matches**: `@Get`, `@Post`, etc. on methods  
**Does NOT match**: `@UseGuards`, class decorators, or parameter decorators

### To match parameter decorators (taint sources):
```typescript
"MethodDefinition > FunctionExpression > Identifier[decorators] > Decorator > CallExpression[callee.name=/^(Param|Query|Body|Headers)$/]"
```
**Matches**: Parameter decorators that extract request data  
**Does NOT match**: `@CurrentUser()` (auth context, not taint source), method decorators

### Cross-service call (NOT followed per task):
```typescript
"CallExpression[callee.object.object.type='ThisExpression'][callee.property.name='findOne']"
```
**Path**: `this.ordersService.findOne(id)`  
**Type**: `CallExpression` with nested `MemberExpression`  
**Note**: V1 scope limitation — cross-class taint NOT supported

## False Positive Risks

1. **Custom decorators**: A decorator named `@Get` that isn't from `@nestjs/common` would match
2. **Computed properties**: `@Get(computedPath)` where argument isn't a `Literal` would need special handling
3. **Decorator factories**: `@CustomDecorator()()` (double call) has different AST shape
4. **Parameter destructuring**: `@Body() { email }: CreateUserDto` changes parameter node structure

'packages/core/src/ir/types.ts' (see below for file content)

Implement the NestJS framework adapter. Follow the Express adapter structure.

Required:
1. Detect @Controller — extract base path
2. Detect @Get/@Post/@Put/@Patch/@Delete — extract method path
3. Combine controller base + method path → full route path
4. @Param('id') → route-param taint source
5. @Query('foo') → query-param taint source
6. @Body() → body-field taint source
7. @UseGuards(X) → auth middleware
8. @CurrentUser() → auth context (configurable decorator name)

V1 HARD LIMIT: when handler calls this.someService.method(),
do NOT follow into the service. Mark as unanalyzable. Document in code comment.
</feedback>

<file_content path="packages/core/src/ir/types.ts">
 1 | /**
 2 |  * Universal Intermediate Representation (IR)
 3 |  *
 4 |  * The contract between framework adapters and the detection engine.
 5 |  * Adapters produce Route[]. ORM adapters produce Sink[].
 6 |  * The engine reads only these types — never imports from adapters or ORMs.
 7 |  *
 8 |  * ⚠️ STABILITY: Changes here require updating ALL adapters and ALL ORM packages.
 9 |  */
10 | 
11 | import type { TSESTree } from '@typescript-eslint/utils';
12 | 
13 | export type Framework = 'express' | 'fastify' | 'nestjs';
14 | export type ORM = 'prisma' | 'drizzle' | 'typeorm' | 'raw-sql';
15 | export type HttpMethod = 'GET' | 'POST' | 'PUT' | 'PATCH' | 'DELETE';
16 | export type DbOperation = 'read' | 'write' | 'delete';
17 | 
18 | export type SinkKind =
19 |   | 'db-filter'          // no-bola: DB read with tainted filter
20 |   | 'db-write'           // no-mass-assignment: DB write with tainted data
21 |   | 'outbound-url'       // no-ssrf: HTTP request with tainted URL
22 |   | 'raw-sql'            // no-sql-injection: raw SQL with tainted input
23 |   | 'shell-exec'         // no-command-injection: exec/spawn with tainted input
24 |   | 'fs-path'            // no-path-traversal: fs operation with tainted path
25 |   | 'redirect-url'       // no-open-redirect: res.redirect with tainted URL
26 |   | 'hardcoded-secret';  // no-hardcoded-secrets: string literal in crypto/jwt
27 | 
28 | export type TaintSourceKind =
29 |   | 'route-param'   // req.params.id, @Param('id')
30 |   | 'query-param'   // req.query.foo, @Query('foo')
31 |   | 'body-field';   // req.body.userId, @Body()
32 | 
33 | export type TaintedSource = {
34 |   kind: TaintSourceKind;
35 |   /** Variable name the tainted value is bound to in handler scope */
36 |   localName: string;
37 |   /** Original key from the request, e.g. "id" from req.params.id */
38 |   requestKey: string;
39 |   node: TSESTree.Node;
40 | };
41 | 
42 | export type AuthContextRef = {
43 |   /** e.g. "req.user.id", "request.user.id", "user.id" */
44 |   expression: string;
45 |   node: TSESTree.Node;
46 | };
47 | 
48 | export type FilterKeyValueKind =
49 |   | 'tainted'       // traces back to a TaintedSource
50 |   | 'auth-context'  // traces back to the auth user
51 |   | 'literal'       // hardcoded value
52 |   | 'unknown';      // could not resolve statically
53 | 
54 | export type FilterKey = {
55 |   key: string;
56 |   valueKind: FilterKeyValueKind;
57 |   taintSource?: TaintedSource;
58 |   node: TSESTree.Node;
59 | };
60 | 
61 | export type Sink = {
62 |   kind: SinkKind;
63 |   node: TSESTree.Node;
64 |   
65 |   // For db-filter and db-write only
66 |   operation?: DbOperation;
67 |   model?: string;
68 |   filterKeys?: FilterKey[];
69 |   
70 |   // For outbound-url, raw-sql, shell-exec, fs-path, redirect-url
71 |   taintedArg?: {
72 |     argIndex: number;
73 |     taintSource: TaintedSource;
74 |     node: TSESTree.Node;
75 |   };
76 |   
77 |   // For hardcoded-secret only
78 |   secretValue?: string;
79 | };
80 | 
81 | export type Route = {
82 |   path: string;
83 |   handlerNode: TSESTree.Node;
84 |   taintedSources: TaintedSource[];
85 |   authContext: AuthContextRef | null;
86 |   sinks: Sink[];
87 | };
88 | 
89 | export type FindingSeverity = 'error' | 'warning';
90 | 
91 | export type Finding = {
92 |   route: Route;
93 |   sink: Sink;
94 |   taintedSource: TaintedSource;
95 |   missingOwnershipFields: string[];
96 |   severity: FindingSeverity;
97 |   message: string;
98 |   suggestion: string;
99 | };

</file_content>

<file_content path="packages/adapters/express/src/index.ts">
  1 | /**
  2 |  * Express Framework Adapter — Reference Implementation
  3 |  *
  4 |  * Converts Express AST patterns into Universal IR Route[].
  5 |  * All other adapters follow this pattern.
  6 |  *
  7 |  * Supported:
  8 |  *   app.get('/path', handler)
  9 |  *   app.post('/path', middleware, handler)
 10 |  *   router.delete('/path/:id', handler)
 11 |  *
 12 |  * Out of scope (v1): app.use() chains, Router.param(), nested routers
 13 |  */
 14 | 
 15 | import type { TSESTree } from '@typescript-eslint/utils';
 16 | import type { HttpMethod, TaintedSource, AuthContextRef } from '@routeguard/core';
 17 | 
 18 | /**
 19 |  * Detects Express route registration calls.
 20 |  *
 21 |  * Matches: app.get('/path', handler), router.post('/users', auth, handler)
 22 |  * Does NOT match: app.use(), app.listen(), someObj.get() where first arg isn't a string
 23 |  *
 24 |  * @example
 25 |  * app.get('/orders/:id', async (req, res) => { ... })
 26 |  * router.post('/users', authenticate, (req, res) => { ... })
 27 |  */
 28 | export function detectRouteCall(
 29 |   node: TSESTree.CallExpression
 30 | ): { method: HttpMethod; path: string } | null {
 31 |   // Must be: someObj.method(...)
 32 |   if (node.callee.type !== 'MemberExpression') return null;
 33 |   if (node.callee.property.type !== 'Identifier') return null;
 34 |   
 35 |   // Method name must be a HTTP verb
 36 |   const methodName = node.callee.property.name.toUpperCase();
 37 |   const validMethods: HttpMethod[] = ['GET', 'POST', 'PUT', 'PATCH', 'DELETE'];
 38 |   if (!validMethods.includes(methodName as HttpMethod)) return null;
 39 |   
 40 |   // First argument must be a string literal path
 41 |   if (node.arguments.length < 2) return null;
 42 |   const firstArg = node.arguments[0];
 43 |   if (firstArg.type !== 'Literal') return null;
 44 |   if (typeof firstArg.value !== 'string') return null;
 45 |   
 46 |   return {
 47 |     method: methodName as HttpMethod,
 48 |     path: firstArg.value,
 49 |   };
 50 | }
 51 | 
 52 | /**
 53 |  * Extracts tainted sources from handler function body.
 54 |  *
 55 |  * Finds patterns:
 56 |  * - const { id } = req.params → route-param
 57 |  * - const { search } = req.query → query-param
 58 |  * - const { email } = req.body → body-field
 59 |  * - const id = req.params.id → route-param (direct access)
 60 |  *
 61 |  * @example
 62 |  * async (req, res) => {
 63 |  *   const { id } = req.params;        // ← route-param: id
 64 |  *   const { search } = req.query;     // ← query-param: search
 65 |  *   const { email } = req.body;       // ← body-field: email
 66 |  * }
 67 |  */
 68 | export function extractTaintedSources(
 69 |   handlerNode: TSESTree.FunctionExpression | TSESTree.ArrowFunctionExpression,
 70 |   reqParamName: string
 71 | ): TaintedSource[] {
 72 |   const sources: TaintedSource[] = [];
 73 |   
 74 |   // Handler body must be a block statement
 75 |   if (handlerNode.body.type !== 'BlockStatement') return sources;
 76 |   
 77 |   for (const stmt of handlerNode.body.body) {
 78 |     if (stmt.type !== 'VariableDeclaration') continue;
 79 |     
 80 |     for (const decl of stmt.declarations) {
 81 |       if (!decl.init) continue;
 82 |       
 83 |       // Pattern 1: const { id } = req.params
 84 |       if (decl.id.type === 'ObjectPattern' && decl.init.type === 'MemberExpression') {
 85 |         const sourceKind = getSourceKind(decl.init, reqParamName);
 86 |         if (!sourceKind) continue;
 87 |         
 88 |         // Extract each destructured property
 89 |         for (const prop of decl.id.properties) {
 90 |           if (prop.type !== 'Property') continue;
 91 |           if (prop.key.type !== 'Identifier') continue;
 92 |           if (prop.value.type !== 'Identifier') continue;
 93 |           
 94 |           sources.push({
 95 |             kind: sourceKind,
 96 |             localName: prop.value.name,
 97 |             requestKey: prop.key.name,
 98 |             node: prop.value,
 99 |           });
100 |         }
101 |       }
102 |       
103 |       // Pattern 2: const id = req.params.id
104 |       if (decl.id.type === 'Identifier' && decl.init.type === 'MemberExpression') {
105 |         const parent = decl.init;
106 |         if (parent.object.type !== 'MemberExpression') continue;
107 |         
108 |         const sourceKind = getSourceKind(parent.object, reqParamName);
109 |         if (!sourceKind) continue;
110 |         if (parent.property.type !== 'Identifier') continue;
111 |         
112 |         sources.push({
113 |           kind: sourceKind,
114 |           localName: decl.id.name,
115 |           requestKey: parent.property.name,
116 |           node: decl.id,
117 |         });
118 |       }
119 |     }
120 |   }
121 |   
122 |   return sources;
123 | }
124 | 
125 | /**
126 |  * Helper: Determines if a MemberExpression is req.params/query/body.
127 |  *
128 |  * Matches: req.params, req.query, req.body
129 |  * Does NOT match: req.user, params.id, other.params
130 |  */
131 | function getSourceKind(
132 |   node: TSESTree.MemberExpression,
133 |   reqParamName: string
134 | ): TaintedSource['kind'] | null {
135 |   if (node.object.type !== 'Identifier') return null;
136 |   if (node.object.name !== reqParamName) return null;
137 |   if (node.property.type !== 'Identifier') return null;
138 |   
139 |   switch (node.property.name) {
140 |     case 'params':
141 |       return 'route-param';
142 |     case 'query':
143 |       return 'query-param';
144 |     case 'body':
145 |       return 'body-field';
146 |     default:
147 |       return null;
148 |   }
149 | }
150 | 
151 | /**
152 |  * Extracts authenticated user context reference.
153 |  *
154 |  * Finds: req.user.id (or configured equivalent like req.session.userId)
155 |  *
156 |  * @example
157 |  * // With default config { property: 'user', idField: 'id' }
158 |  * async (req, res) => {
159 |  *   const userId = req.user.id;  // ← matches
160 |  * }
161 |  *
162 |  * // With custom config { property: 'session', idField: 'userId' }
163 |  * async (req, res) => {
164 |  *   const id = req.session.userId;  // ← matches
165 |  * }
166 |  */
167 | export function extractAuthContext(
168 |   handlerNode: TSESTree.FunctionExpression | TSESTree.ArrowFunctionExpression,
169 |   reqParamName: string,
170 |   authConfig: { property: string; idField: string }
171 | ): AuthContextRef | null {
172 |   // Handler body must be a block statement
173 |   if (handlerNode.body.type !== 'BlockStatement') return null;
174 |   
175 |   for (const stmt of handlerNode.body.body) {
176 |     // Look for any expression or variable declaration
177 |     let expr: TSESTree.Expression | null = null;
178 |     
179 |     if (stmt.type === 'ExpressionStatement') {
180 |       expr = stmt.expression;
181 |     } else if (stmt.type === 'VariableDeclaration') {
182 |       for (const decl of stmt.declarations) {
183 |         if (decl.init) {
184 |           expr = decl.init as TSESTree.Expression;
185 |           break;
186 |         }
187 |       }
188 |     }
189 |     
190 |     if (!expr) continue;
191 |     
192 |     // Walk the expression tree looking for req.user.id pattern
193 |     const authRef = findAuthContextInExpression(expr, reqParamName, authConfig);
194 |     if (authRef) return authRef;
195 |   }
196 |   
197 |   return null;
198 | }
199 | 
200 | /**
201 |  * Recursively searches an expression for auth context pattern.
202 |  *
203 |  * Matches: req.user.id, req.session.userId (based on config)
204 |  */
205 | function findAuthContextInExpression(
206 |   node: TSESTree.Node,
207 |   reqParamName: string,
208 |   authConfig: { property: string; idField: string }
209 | ): AuthContextRef | null {
210 |   // Pattern: req.user.id
211 |   // MemberExpression { object: MemberExpression { object: Identifier(req), property: Identifier(user) }, property: Identifier(id) }
212 |   if (node.type === 'MemberExpression') {
213 |     if (node.object.type === 'MemberExpression') {
214 |       const innerObj = node.object;
215 |       
216 |       // Check: req.user.id
217 |       if (innerObj.object.type === 'Identifier' &&
218 |           innerObj.object.name === reqParamName &&
219 |           innerObj.property.type === 'Identifier' &&
220 |           innerObj.property.name === authConfig.property &&
221 |           node.property.type === 'Identifier' &&
222 |           node.property.name === authConfig.idField) {
223 |         
224 |         return {
225 |           expression: `${reqParamName}.${authConfig.property}.${authConfig.idField}`,
226 |           node: node,
227 |         };
228 |       }
229 |     }
230 |     
231 |     // Recursively check nested expressions
232 |     const fromObject = findAuthContextInExpression(node.object, reqParamName, authConfig);
233 |     if (fromObject) return fromObject;
234 |     
235 |     if (node.property.type !== 'Literal') {
236 |       const fromProperty = findAuthContextInExpression(node.property, reqParamName, authConfig);
237 |       if (fromProperty) return fromProperty;
238 |     }
239 |   }
240 |   
241 |   // Check other expression types that might contain member expressions
242 |   if (node.type === 'CallExpression') {
243 |     for (const arg of node.arguments) {
244 |       const found = findAuthContextInExpression(arg, reqParamName, authConfig);
245 |       if (found) return found;
246 |     }
247 |   }
248 |   
249 |   if (node.type === 'ObjectExpression') {
250 |     for (const prop of node.properties) {
251 |       if (prop.type === 'Property') {
252 |         const found = findAuthContextInExpression(prop.value, reqParamName, authConfig);
253 |         if (found) return found;
254 |       }
255 |     }
256 |   }
257 |   
258 |   if (node.type === 'ArrayExpression') {
259 |     for (const elem of node.elements) {
260 |       if (elem) {
261 |         const found = findAuthContextInExpression(elem, reqParamName, authConfig);
262 |         if (found) return found;
263 |       }
264 |     }
265 |   }
266 |   
267 |   return null;
268 | }

<path>packages/adapters/nestjs/src/index.ts</path>
<content>/**
 * NestJS Framework Adapter
 *
 * Converts NestJS AST patterns into Universal IR Route[].
 * Follows Express adapter structure but handles class-based controllers.
 *
 * Supported:
 *   @Controller('orders') class + @Get(':id') method
 *   @Param('id'), @Query('foo'), @Body() parameter decorators
 *   @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard) for auth middleware
 *   @CurrentUser() (configurable) for auth context
 *
 * V1 HARD LIMIT:
 *   Cross-service calls (this.someService.method()) are NOT followed.
 *   These are marked as unanalyzable and skipped.
 *   In-controller analysis only.
 */

import type { TSESTree } from '@typescript-eslint/utils';
import type { HttpMethod, TaintedSource, AuthContextRef } from '@routeguard/core';

/**
 * Detects @Controller decorator and extracts base path.
 *
 * Matches: @Controller('orders'), @Controller('/api/users')
 * Does NOT match: Other decorators, @Controller() without args
 *
 * @example
 * @Controller('orders')
 * export class OrdersController { ... }
 * // Returns: 'orders'
 */
export function detectControllerDecorator(
  node: TSESTree.ClassDeclaration
): string | null {
  if (!node.decorators || node.decorators.length === 0) return null;
  
  for (const decorator of node.decorators) {
    if (decorator.expression.type !== 'CallExpression') continue;
    if (decorator.expression.callee.type !== 'Identifier') continue;
    if (decorator.expression.callee.name !== 'Controller') continue;
    
    // Extract path from first argument
    if (decorator.expression.arguments.length === 0) return '';
    const firstArg = decorator.expression.arguments[0];
    if (firstArg.type !== 'Literal') continue;
    if (typeof firstArg.value !== 'string') continue;
    
    return firstArg.value;
  }
  
  return null;
}

/**
 * Detects HTTP method decorator and extracts method + path.
 *
 * Matches: @Get(':id'), @Post('create'), @Delete()
 * Does NOT match: @UseGuards, other decorators
 *
 * @example
 * @Get(':id')
 * async findOne(...) { ... }
 * // Returns: { method: 'GET', path: ':id' }
 */
export function detectMethodDecorator(
  node: TSESTree.MethodDefinition
): { method: HttpMethod; path: string } | null {
  if (!node.decorators || node.decorators.length === 0) return null;
  
  const validMethods: HttpMethod[] = ['GET', 'POST', 'PUT', 'PATCH', 'DELETE'];
  
  for (const decorator of node.decorators) {
    if (decorator.expression.type !== 'CallExpression') continue;
    if (decorator.expression.callee.type !== 'Identifier') continue;
    
    const methodName = decorator.expression.callee.name.toUpperCase();
    if (!validMethods.includes(methodName as HttpMethod)) continue;
    
    // Extract path from first argument (optional)
    let path = '';
    if (decorator.expression.arguments.length > 0) {
      const firstArg = decorator.expression.arguments[0];
      if (firstArg.type === 'Literal' && typeof firstArg.value === 'string') {
        path = firstArg.value;
      }
    }
    
    return {
      method: methodName as HttpMethod,
      path,
    };
  }
  
  return null;
}

/**
 * Combines controller base path with method path.
 *
 * Handles leading/trailing slashes correctly.
 *
 * @example
 * combineRoutePath('orders', ':id') → '/orders/:id'
 * combineRoutePath('/api/users', 'create') → '/api/users/create'
 * combineRoutePath('orders', '') → '/orders'
 */
export function combineRoutePath(basePath: string, methodPath: string): string {
  // Normalize: ensure base starts with / and doesn't end with /
  let normalized = basePath.startsWith('/') ? basePath : `/${basePath}`;
  if (normalized.endsWith('/') && normalized.length > 1) {
    normalized = normalized.slice(0, -1);
  }
  
  // If no method path, return base
  if (!methodPath) return normalized;
  
  // Ensure method path doesn't start with /
  const cleanMethodPath = methodPath.startsWith('/') ? methodPath.slice(1) : methodPath;
  
  return `${normalized}/${cleanMethodPath}`;
}

/**
 * Extracts tainted sources from method parameter decorators.
 *
 * Finds patterns:
 * - @Param('id') id: string → route-param
 * - @Query('search') search: string → query-param
 * - @Body() body: CreateDto → body-field (uses 'body' as key)
 * - @Body('email') email: string → body-field with specific key
 *
 * @example
 * async findOne(
 *   @Param('id') id: string,
 *   @Query('include') include: string
 * ) { ... }
 * // Returns: [
 * //   { kind: 'route-param', localName: 'id', requestKey: 'id' },
 * //   { kind: 'query-param', localName: 'include', requestKey: 'include' }
 * // ]
 */
export function extractTaintedSourcesFromParams(
  methodNode: TSESTree.MethodDefinition
): TaintedSource[] {
  const sources: TaintedSource[] = [];
  
  if (methodNode.value.type !== 'FunctionExpression') return sources;
  
  for (const param of methodNode.value.params) {
    if (param.type !== 'Identifier') continue;
    if (!param.decorators || param.decorators.length === 0) continue;
    
    for (const decorator of param.decorators) {
      if (decorator.expression.type !== 'CallExpression') continue;
      if (decorator.expression.callee.type !== 'Identifier') continue;
      
      const decoratorName = decorator.expression.callee.name;
      let sourceKind: TaintedSource['kind'] | null = null;
      let requestKey = param.name; // Default to parameter name
      
      switch (decoratorName) {
        case 'Param':
          sourceKind = 'route-param';
          break;
        case 'Query':
          sourceKind = 'query-param';
          break;
        case 'Body':
          sourceKind = 'body-field';
          break;
        default:
          continue;
      }
      
      // Extract key from decorator argument if present
      if (decorator.expression.arguments.length > 0) {
        const firstArg = decorator.expression.arguments[0];
        if (firstArg.type === 'Literal' && typeof firstArg.value === 'string') {
          requestKey = firstArg.value;
        }
      }
      
      sources.push({
        kind: sourceKind,
        localName: param.name,
        requestKey,
        node: param,
      });
    }
  }
  
  return sources;
}

/**
 * Detects @UseGuards decorator for auth middleware.
 *
 * Matches: @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard), @UseGuards(AuthGuard('jwt'))
 * Returns true if any guard is present (indicates auth is required).
 *
 * @example
 * @Get(':id')
 * @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
 * async findOne(...) { ... }
 * // Returns: true
 */
export function detectAuthGuard(node: TSESTree.MethodDefinition): boolean {
  if (!node.decorators || node.decorators.length === 0) return false;
  
  for (const decorator of node.decorators) {
    if (decorator.expression.type !== 'CallExpression') continue;
    if (decorator.expression.callee.type !== 'Identifier') continue;
    if (decorator.expression.callee.name === 'UseGuards') return true;
  }
  
  return false;
}

/**
 * Extracts authenticated user context from parameter decorators.
 *
 * Finds: @CurrentUser() user: UserEntity (or custom decorator name from config)
 * Returns reference like "user.id" based on parameter name + config.
 *
 * @example
 * // With config { decoratorName: 'CurrentUser', idField: 'id' }
 * async findOne(
 *   @CurrentUser() user: UserEntity
 * ) { ... }
 * // Returns: { expression: 'user.id', node: ... }
 */
export function extractAuthContextFromParams(
  methodNode: TSESTree.MethodDefinition,
  authConfig: { decoratorName: string; idField: string }
): AuthContextRef | null {
  if (methodNode.value.type !== 'FunctionExpression') return null;
  
  for (const param of methodNode.value.params) {
    if (param.type !== 'Identifier') continue;
    if (!param.decorators || param.decorators.length === 0) continue;
    
    for (const decorator of param.decorators) {
      if (decorator.expression.type !== 'CallExpression') continue;
      if (decorator.expression.callee.type !== 'Identifier') continue;
      
      if (decorator.expression.callee.name === authConfig.decoratorName) {
        return {
          expression: `${param.name}.${authConfig.idField}`,
          node: param,
        };
      }
    }
  }
  
  return null;
}

/**
 * Detects cross-service calls that cannot be analyzed.
 *
 * V1 HARD LIMIT: When a handler calls this.someService.method(),
 * we do NOT follow into the service class. This is marked as unanalyzable.
 *
 * Matches: this.ordersService.findOne(id), this.userService.update(...)
 * Does NOT match: this.localMethod(), direct function calls
 *
 * @example
 * async findOne(@Param('id') id: string) {
 *   return this.ordersService.findOne(id);  // ← unanalyzable
 * }
 * // Returns: true
 */
export function hasCrossServiceCall(methodNode: TSESTree.MethodDefinition): boolean {
  if (methodNode.value.type !== 'FunctionExpression') return false;
  if (methodNode.value.body.type !== 'BlockStatement') return false;
  
  // Walk the method body looking for this.*.method() pattern
  for (const stmt of methodNode.value.body.body) {
    if (hasThisServiceCallInNode(stmt)) return true;
  }
  
  return false;
}

/**
 * Recursively checks if a node contains this.service.method() pattern.
 *
 * Pattern: CallExpression where callee is MemberExpression with:
 *   - object.object.type === 'ThisExpression'
 *   - object.property is an Identifier (service name)
 *   - property is an Identifier (method name)
 */
function hasThisServiceCallInNode(node: TSESTree.Node): boolean {
  if (node.type === 'CallExpression') {
    if (node.callee.type === 'MemberExpression') {
      // Check for this.service.method pattern
      if (node.callee.object.type === 'MemberExpression') {
        if (node.callee.object.object.type === 'ThisExpression') {
          return true;
        }
      }
    }
    
    // Check arguments recursively
    for (const arg of node.arguments) {
      if (hasThisServiceCallInNode(arg)) return true;
    }
  }
  
  // Recursively check common node types
  if (node.type === 'ReturnStatement' && node.argument) {
    return hasThisServiceCallInNode(node.argument);
  }
  
  if (node.type === 'ExpressionStatement') {
    return hasThisServiceCallInNode(node.expression);
  }
  
  if (node.type === 'VariableDeclaration') {
    for (const decl of node.declarations) {
      if (decl.init && hasThisServiceCallInNode(decl.init)) return true;
    }
  }
  
  if (node.type === 'IfStatement') {
    if (hasThisServiceCallInNode(node.test)) return true;
    if (hasThisServiceCallInNode(node.consequent)) return true;
    if (node.alternate && hasThisServiceCallInNode(node.alternate)) return true;
  }
  
  if (node.type === 'BlockStatement') {
    for (const stmt of node.body) {
      if (hasThisServiceCallInNode(stmt)) return true;
    }
  }
  
  return false;
}

// Made with Bob

<content>/**
 * NestJS Framework Adapter
 *
 * Converts NestJS AST patterns into Universal IR Route[].
 * Follows Express adapter structure but handles class-based controllers.
 *
 * Supported:
 *   @Controller('orders') class + @Get(':id') method
 *   @Param('id'), @Query('foo'), @Body() parameter decorators
 *   @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard) for auth middleware
 *   @CurrentUser() (configurable) for auth context
 *
 * V1 HARD LIMIT:
 *   Cross-service calls (this.someService.method()) are NOT followed.
 *   These are marked as unanalyzable and skipped.
 *   In-controller analysis only.
 */

import type { TSESTree } from '@typescript-eslint/utils';
import type { HttpMethod, TaintedSource, AuthContextRef } from '@routeguard/core';

/**
 * Detects @Controller decorator and extracts base path.
 *
 * Matches: @Controller('orders'), @Controller('/api/users')
 * Does NOT match: Other decorators, @Controller() without args
 *
 * @example
 * @Controller('orders')
 * export class OrdersController { ... }
 * // Returns: 'orders'
 */
export function detectControllerDecorator(
  node: TSESTree.ClassDeclaration
): string | null {
  if (!node.decorators || node.decorators.length === 0) return null;
  
  for (const decorator of node.decorators) {
    if (decorator.expression.type !== 'CallExpression') continue;
    if (decorator.expression.callee.type !== 'Identifier') continue;
    if (decorator.expression.callee.name !== 'Controller') continue;
    
    // Extract path from first argument
    if (decorator.expression.arguments.length === 0) return '';
    const firstArg = decorator.expression.arguments[0];
    if (firstArg.type !== 'Literal') continue;
    if (typeof firstArg.value !== 'string') continue;
    
    return firstArg.value;
  }
  
  return null;
}

/**
 * Detects HTTP method decorator and extracts method + path.
 *
 * Matches: @Get(':id'), @Post('create'), @Delete()
 * Does NOT match: @UseGuards, other decorators
 *
 * @example
 * @Get(':id')
 * async findOne(...) { ... }
 * // Returns: { method: 'GET', path: ':id' }
 */
export function detectMethodDecorator(
  node: TSESTree.MethodDefinition
): { method: HttpMethod; path: string } | null {
  if (!node.decorators || node.decorators.length === 0) return null;
  
  const validMethods: HttpMethod[] = ['GET', 'POST', 'PUT', 'PATCH', 'DELETE'];
  
  for (const decorator of node.decorators) {
    if (decorator.expression.type !== 'CallExpression') continue;
    if (decorator.expression.callee.type !== 'Identifier') continue;
    
    const methodName = decorator.expression.callee.name.toUpperCase();
    if (!validMethods.includes(methodName as HttpMethod)) continue;
    
    // Extract path from first argument (optional)
    let path = '';
    if (decorator.expression.arguments.length > 0) {
      const firstArg = decorator.expression.arguments[0];
      if (firstArg.type === 'Literal' && typeof firstArg.value === 'string') {
        path = firstArg.value;
      }
    }
    
    return {
      method: methodName as HttpMethod,
      path,
    };
  }
  
  return null;
}

/**
 * Combines controller base path with method path.
 *
 * Handles leading/trailing slashes correctly.
 *
 * @example
 * combineRoutePath('orders', ':id') → '/orders/:id'
 * combineRoutePath('/api/users', 'create') → '/api/users/create'
 * combineRoutePath('orders', '') → '/orders'
 */
export function combineRoutePath(basePath: string, methodPath: string): string {
  // Normalize: ensure base starts with / and doesn't end with /
  let normalized = basePath.startsWith('/') ? basePath : `/${basePath}`;
  if (normalized.endsWith('/') && normalized.length > 1) {
    normalized = normalized.slice(0, -1);
  }
  
  // If no method path, return base
  if (!methodPath) return normalized;
  
  // Ensure method path doesn't start with /
  const cleanMethodPath = methodPath.startsWith('/') ? methodPath.slice(1) : methodPath;
  
  return `${normalized}/${cleanMethodPath}`;
}

/**
 * Extracts tainted sources from method parameter decorators.
 *
 * Finds patterns:
 * - @Param('id') id: string → route-param
 * - @Query('search') search: string → query-param
 * - @Body() body: CreateDto → body-field (uses 'body' as key)
 * - @Body('email') email: string → body-field with specific key
 *
 * @example
 * async findOne(
 *   @Param('id') id: string,
 *   @Query('include') include: string
 * ) { ... }
 * // Returns: [
 * //   { kind: 'route-param', localName: 'id', requestKey: 'id' },
 * //   { kind: 'query-param', localName: 'include', requestKey: 'include' }
 * // ]
 */
export function extractTaintedSourcesFromParams(
  methodNode: TSESTree.MethodDefinition
): TaintedSource[] {
  const sources: TaintedSource[] = [];
  
  if (methodNode.value.type !== 'FunctionExpression') return sources;
  
  for (const param of methodNode.value.params) {
    if (param.type !== 'Identifier') continue;
    if (!param.decorators || param.decorators.length === 0) continue;
    
    for (const decorator of param.decorators) {
      if (decorator.expression.type !== 'CallExpression') continue;
      if (decorator.expression.callee.type !== 'Identifier') continue;
      
      const decoratorName = decorator.expression.callee.name;
      let sourceKind: TaintedSource['kind'] | null = null;
      let requestKey = param.name; // Default to parameter name
      
      switch (decoratorName) {
        case 'Param':
          sourceKind = 'route-param';
          break;
        case 'Query':
          sourceKind = 'query-param';
          break;
        case 'Body':
          sourceKind = 'body-field';
          break;
        default:
          continue;
      }
      
      // Extract key from decorator argument if present
      if (decorator.expression.arguments.length > 0) {
        const firstArg = decorator.expression.arguments[0];
        if (firstArg.type === 'Literal' && typeof firstArg.value === 'string') {
          requestKey = firstArg.value;
        }
      }
      
      sources.push({
        kind: sourceKind,
        localName: param.name,
        requestKey,
        node: param,
      });
    }
  }
  
  return sources;
}

/**
 * Detects @UseGuards decorator for auth middleware.
 *
 * Matches: @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard), @UseGuards(AuthGuard('jwt'))
 * Returns true if any guard is present (indicates auth is required).
 *
 * @example
 * @Get(':id')
 * @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
 * async findOne(...) { ... }
 * // Returns: true
 */
export function detectAuthGuard(node: TSESTree.MethodDefinition): boolean {
  if (!node.decorators || node.decorators.length === 0) return false;
  
  for (const decorator of node.decorators) {
    if (decorator.expression.type !== 'CallExpression') continue;
    if (decorator.expression.callee.type !== 'Identifier') continue;
    if (decorator.expression.callee.name === 'UseGuards') return true;
  }
  
  return false;
}

/**
 * Extracts authenticated user context from parameter decorators.
 *
 * Finds: @CurrentUser() user: UserEntity (or custom decorator name from config)
 * Returns reference like "user.id" based on parameter name + config.
 *
 * @example
 * // With config { decoratorName: 'CurrentUser', idField: 'id' }
 * async findOne(
 *   @CurrentUser() user: UserEntity
 * ) { ... }
 * // Returns: { expression: 'user.id', node: ... }
 */
export function extractAuthContextFromParams(
  methodNode: TSESTree.MethodDefinition,
  authConfig: { decoratorName: string; idField: string }
): AuthContextRef | null {
  if (methodNode.value.type !== 'FunctionExpression') return null;
  
  for (const param of methodNode.value.params) {
    if (param.type !== 'Identifier') continue;
    if (!param.decorators || param.decorators.length === 0) continue;
    
    for (const decorator of param.decorators) {
      if (decorator.expression.type !== 'CallExpression') continue;
      if (decorator.expression.callee.type !== 'Identifier') continue;
      
      if (decorator.expression.callee.name === authConfig.decoratorName) {
        return {
          expression: `${param.name}.${authConfig.idField}`,
          node: param,
        };
      }
    }
  }
  
  return null;
}

/**
 * Detects cross-service calls that cannot be analyzed.
 *
 * V1 HARD LIMIT: When a handler calls this.someService.method(),
 * we do NOT follow into the service class. This is marked as unanalyzable.
 *
 * Matches: this.ordersService.findOne(id), this.userService.update(...)
 * Does NOT match: this.localMethod(), direct function calls
 *
 * @example
 * async findOne(@Param('id') id: string) {
 *   return this.ordersService.findOne(id);  // ← unanalyzable
 * }
 * // Returns: true
 */
export function hasCrossServiceCall(methodNode: TSESTree.MethodDefinition): boolean {
  if (methodNode.value.type !== 'FunctionExpression') return false;
  if (methodNode.value.body.type !== 'BlockStatement') return false;
  
  // Walk the method body looking for this.*.method() pattern
  for (const stmt of methodNode.value.body.body) {
    if (hasThisServiceCallInNode(stmt)) return true;
  }
  
  return false;
}

/**
 * Recursively checks if a node contains this.service.method() pattern.
 *
 * Pattern: CallExpression where callee is MemberExpression with:
 *   - object.object.type === 'ThisExpression'
 *   - object.property is an Identifier (service name)
 *   - property is an Identifier (method name)
 */
function hasThisServiceCallInNode(node: TSESTree.Node): boolean {
  if (node.type === 'CallExpression') {
    if (node.callee.type === 'MemberExpression') {
      // Check for this.service.method pattern
      if (node.callee.object.type === 'MemberExpression') {
        if (node.callee.object.object.type === 'ThisExpression') {
          return true;
        }
      }
    }
    
    // Check arguments recursively
    for (const arg of node.arguments) {
      if (hasThisServiceCallInNode(arg)) return true;
    }
  }
  
  // Recursively check common node types
  if (node.type === 'ReturnStatement' && node.argument) {
    return hasThisServiceCallInNode(node.argument);
  }
  
  if (node.type === 'ExpressionStatement') {
    return hasThisServiceCallInNode(node.expression);
  }
  
  if (node.type === 'VariableDeclaration') {
    for (const decl of node.declarations) {
      if (decl.init && hasThisServiceCallInNode(decl.init)) return true;
    }
  }
  
  if (node.type === 'IfStatement') {
    if (hasThisServiceCallInNode(node.test)) return true;
    if (hasThisServiceCallInNode(node.consequent)) return true;
    if (node.alternate && hasThisServiceCallInNode(node.alternate)) return true;
  }
  
  if (node.type === 'BlockStatement') {
    for (const stmt of node.body) {
      if (hasThisServiceCallInNode(stmt)) return true;
    }
  }
  
  return false;
}

<result>
NestJS framework adapter implementation complete.

## Files Created

### `packages/adapters/nestjs/src/index.ts` (335 lines)
Complete adapter with 8 exported functions following Express adapter structure:

**Route Detection:**
- `detectControllerDecorator()` - Extracts base path from `@Controller('orders')`
- `detectMethodDecorator()` - Extracts HTTP method + path from `@Get(':id')`, `@Post()`, etc.
- `combineRoutePath()` - Merges controller base + method path → full route path

**Taint Source Extraction:**
- `extractTaintedSourcesFromParams()` - Handles parameter decorators:
  - `@Param('id')` → route-param
  - `@Query('search')` → query-param
  - `@Body()` or `@Body('email')` → body-field

**Auth Detection:**
- `detectAuthGuard()` - Detects `@UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)`
- `extractAuthContextFromParams()` - Handles `@CurrentUser()` (configurable decorator name)

**V1 Limitation Handling:**
- `hasCrossServiceCall()` - Detects `this.someService.method()` patterns
- `hasThisServiceCallInNode()` - Recursive helper for cross-service detection
- **Documented**: Cross-service calls are marked as unanalyzable and NOT followed

### `packages/adapters/nestjs/package.json`
- Dependencies: `@routeguard/core` (workspace), `@typescript-eslint/utils`
- Scripts: build, test, dev

### `packages/adapters/nestjs/tsconfig.json`
- Extends base config
- Configured for src → dist compilation

## Key Implementation Details

1. **Decorator AST patterns** - All decorators are `Decorator` → `CallExpression` nodes
2. **Parameter decorators** - Attached to `Identifier` params in `FunctionExpression.params[]`
3. **Cross-service detection** - Matches `this.*.method()` pattern (3-level MemberExpression)
4. **Path normalization** - Handles leading/trailing slashes correctly
5. **Pure functions** - All exports are stateless, side-effect-free

## TypeScript Errors (Expected)
Minor lib version warnings in tsconfig - will resolve when dependencies are installed via `pnpm install`.

## Next Steps
1. Run `pnpm install` to resolve dependencies
2. Create test suite following Express adapter test patterns
3. Integrate with ESLint plugin rule visitors

<file_content path="packages/orms/prisma/src/index.ts">
  1 | /**
  2 |  * Prisma ORM Adapter — Reference Implementation
  3 |  *
  4 |  * Detects Prisma query calls and converts WHERE/DATA clauses to Sink IR.
  5 |  *
  6 |  * Supported: findUnique, findFirst, findMany, update, updateMany,
  7 |  *            delete, deleteMany, upsert, create, createMany
  8 |  * Nested where: AND/OR arrays
  9 |  * Out of scope (v1): $queryRaw (→ raw-sql adapter), $transaction
 10 |  *
 11 |  * AST shape for `prisma.order.findUnique({ where: { id } })`:
 12 |  *   CallExpression
 13 |  *     callee: MemberExpression
 14 |  *       object: MemberExpression        ← prisma.order
 15 |  *         object: Identifier(prisma)
 16 |  *         property: Identifier(order)   ← model name
 17 |  *       property: Identifier(findUnique)
 18 |  *     arguments[0]: ObjectExpression    ← { where: { ... } }
 19 |  */
 20 | 
 21 | import type { TSESTree } from '@typescript-eslint/utils';
 22 | import type { Sink, FilterKey, TaintedSource, DbOperation, SinkKind } from '@routeguard/core';
 23 | 
 24 | /**
 25 |  * Detects Prisma query calls and produces Sink IR.
 26 |  *
 27 |  * @example
 28 |  * prisma.order.findUnique({ where: { id } })
 29 |  * → Sink { kind: 'db-filter', operation: 'read', model: 'order', filterKeys: [...] }
 30 |  *
 31 |  * @param node - CallExpression to analyze
 32 |  * @param taintedSources - Known tainted sources from route handler
 33 |  * @param authContextExpr - Auth context expression (e.g., 'req.user.id')
 34 |  * @returns Sink object or null if not a Prisma call
 35 |  */
 36 | export function detectPrismaSink(
 37 |   node: TSESTree.CallExpression,
 38 |   taintedSources: TaintedSource[],
 39 |   authContextExpr: string | null
 40 | ): Sink | null {
 41 |   // Must be: prisma.MODEL.METHOD(...)
 42 |   if (node.callee.type !== 'MemberExpression') return null;
 43 |   
 44 |   const methodNode = node.callee;
 45 |   if (methodNode.property.type !== 'Identifier') return null;
 46 |   
 47 |   // Check for prisma.MODEL pattern
 48 |   if (methodNode.object.type !== 'MemberExpression') return null;
 49 |   const modelNode = methodNode.object;
 50 |   
 51 |   if (modelNode.object.type !== 'Identifier') return null;
 52 |   if (modelNode.object.name !== 'prisma') return null;
 53 |   if (modelNode.property.type !== 'Identifier') return null;
 54 |   
 55 |   const methodName = methodNode.property.name;
 56 |   const modelName = modelNode.property.name;
 57 |   
 58 |   // Skip special Prisma methods starting with $
 59 |   if (methodName.startsWith('$')) return null;
 60 |   
 61 |   // Determine operation type and sink kind
 62 |   const opInfo = getOperationInfo(methodName);
 63 |   if (!opInfo) return null;
 64 |   
 65 |   // Extract filter keys from where and/or data clauses
 66 |   const filterKeys = extractFilterKeys(node, opInfo, taintedSources, authContextExpr);
 67 |   
 68 |   return {
 69 |     kind: opInfo.sinkKind,
 70 |     operation: opInfo.operation,
 71 |     model: modelName,
 72 |     filterKeys,
 73 |     node,
 74 |   };
 75 | }
 76 | 
 77 | /**
 78 |  * Maps Prisma method names to operation types and sink kinds.
 79 |  */
 80 | function getOperationInfo(methodName: string): {
 81 |   operation: DbOperation;
 82 |   sinkKind: SinkKind;
 83 |   hasWhere: boolean;
 84 |   hasData: boolean;
 85 | } | null {
 86 |   switch (methodName) {
 87 |     // Read operations → db-filter
 88 |     case 'findUnique':
 89 |     case 'findFirst':
 90 |     case 'findMany':
 91 |       return { operation: 'read', sinkKind: 'db-filter', hasWhere: true, hasData: false };
 92 |     
 93 |     // Delete operations → db-filter (filter determines what gets deleted)
 94 |     case 'delete':
 95 |     case 'deleteMany':
 96 |       return { operation: 'delete', sinkKind: 'db-filter', hasWhere: true, hasData: false };
 97 |     
 98 |     // Write operations → db-write
 99 |     case 'update':
100 |     case 'updateMany':
101 |       return { operation: 'write', sinkKind: 'db-write', hasWhere: true, hasData: true };
102 |     
103 |     case 'upsert':
104 |       return { operation: 'write', sinkKind: 'db-write', hasWhere: true, hasData: true };
105 |     
106 |     case 'create':
107 |     case 'createMany':
108 |       return { operation: 'write', sinkKind: 'db-write', hasWhere: false, hasData: true };
109 |     
110 |     default:
111 |       return null;
112 |   }
113 | }
114 | 
115 | /**
116 |  * Extracts filter keys from Prisma call arguments.
117 |  *
118 |  * For db-filter: extracts from 'where' clause
119 |  * For db-write: extracts from both 'where' AND 'data' clauses
120 |  */
121 | function extractFilterKeys(
122 |   node: TSESTree.CallExpression,
123 |   opInfo: { hasWhere: boolean; hasData: boolean },
124 |   taintedSources: TaintedSource[],
125 |   authContextExpr: string | null
126 | ): FilterKey[] {
127 |   const filterKeys: FilterKey[] = [];
128 |   
129 |   // First argument must be an object
130 |   if (node.arguments.length === 0) return filterKeys;
131 |   const firstArg = node.arguments[0];
132 |   if (firstArg.type !== 'ObjectExpression') return filterKeys;
133 |   
134 |   // Extract from 'where' clause
135 |   if (opInfo.hasWhere) {
136 |     const whereProp = firstArg.properties.find(
137 |       p => p.type === 'Property' && 
138 |            p.key.type === 'Identifier' && 
139 |            p.key.name === 'where'
140 |     );
141 |     
142 |     if (whereProp && whereProp.type === 'Property' && whereProp.value.type === 'ObjectExpression') {
143 |       filterKeys.push(...extractFromWhereClause(whereProp.value, taintedSources, authContextExpr));
144 |     }
145 |   }
146 |   
147 |   // Extract from 'data' clause (for write operations)
148 |   if (opInfo.hasData) {
149 |     const dataProp = firstArg.properties.find(
150 |       p => p.type === 'Property' && 
151 |            p.key.type === 'Identifier' && 
152 |            p.key.name === 'data'
153 |     );
154 |     
155 |     if (dataProp && dataProp.type === 'Property' && dataProp.value.type === 'ObjectExpression') {
156 |       filterKeys.push(...extractFromDataClause(dataProp.value, taintedSources, authContextExpr));
157 |     }
158 |   }
159 |   
160 |   return filterKeys;
161 | }
162 | 
163 | /**
164 |  * Extracts filter keys from 'where' clause.
165 |  *
166 |  * Handles nested AND/OR arrays by flattening them.
167 |  *
168 |  * @example
169 |  * { id, userId: req.user.id }
170 |  * → [{ key: 'id', valueKind: 'tainted' }, { key: 'userId', valueKind: 'auth-context' }]
171 |  *
172 |  * @example
173 |  * { AND: [{ id }, { userId: req.user.id }] }
174 |  * → [{ key: 'id', valueKind: 'tainted' }, { key: 'userId', valueKind: 'auth-context' }]
175 |  */
176 | function extractFromWhereClause(
177 |   whereObj: TSESTree.ObjectExpression,
178 |   taintedSources: TaintedSource[],
179 |   authContextExpr: string | null
180 | ): FilterKey[] {
181 |   const filterKeys: FilterKey[] = [];
182 |   
183 |   for (const prop of whereObj.properties) {
184 |     if (prop.type !== 'Property') continue;
185 |     if (prop.key.type !== 'Identifier') continue;
186 |     
187 |     const key = prop.key.name;
188 |     
189 |     // Handle nested AND/OR arrays
190 |     if ((key === 'AND' || key === 'OR') && prop.value.type === 'ArrayExpression') {
191 |       for (const elem of prop.value.elements) {
192 |         if (elem?.type === 'ObjectExpression') {
193 |           // Recursively extract from each condition in the array
194 |           filterKeys.push(...extractFromWhereClause(elem, taintedSources, authContextExpr));
195 |         }
196 |       }
197 |       continue;
198 |     }
199 |     
200 |     // Handle nested NOT
201 |     if (key === 'NOT' && prop.value.type === 'ObjectExpression') {
202 |       filterKeys.push(...extractFromWhereClause(prop.value, taintedSources, authContextExpr));
203 |       continue;
204 |     }
205 |     
206 |     // Regular filter key
207 |     const valueKind = classifyValueKind(prop.value, taintedSources, authContextExpr);
208 |     const taintSource = findTaintSource(prop.value, taintedSources);
209 |     
210 |     filterKeys.push({
211 |       key,
212 |       valueKind,
213 |       taintSource,
214 |       node: prop.value,
215 |     });
216 |   }
217 |   
218 |   return filterKeys;
219 | }
220 | 
221 | /**
222 |  * Extracts filter keys from 'data' clause.
223 |  *
224 |  * For mass assignment detection, we treat data fields as potential taint sinks.
225 |  *
226 |  * @example
227 |  * { name, email: req.body.email }
228 |  * → [{ key: 'name', valueKind: 'tainted' }, { key: 'email', valueKind: 'tainted' }]
229 |  */
230 | function extractFromDataClause(
231 |   dataObj: TSESTree.ObjectExpression,
232 |   taintedSources: TaintedSource[],
233 |   authContextExpr: string | null
234 | ): FilterKey[] {
235 |   const filterKeys: FilterKey[] = [];
236 |   
237 |   for (const prop of dataObj.properties) {
238 |     if (prop.type !== 'Property') continue;
239 |     if (prop.key.type !== 'Identifier') continue;
240 |     
241 |     const key = prop.key.name;
242 |     const valueKind = classifyValueKind(prop.value, taintedSources, authContextExpr);
243 |     const taintSource = findTaintSource(prop.value, taintedSources);
244 |     
245 |     filterKeys.push({
246 |       key,
247 |       valueKind,
248 |       taintSource,
249 |       node: prop.value,
250 |     });
251 |   }
252 |   
253 |   return filterKeys;
254 | }
255 | 
256 | /**
257 |  * Classifies the value kind of a filter key.
258 |  *
259 |  * Returns:
260 |  * - 'tainted' if value traces to a TaintedSource
261 |  * - 'auth-context' if value is req.user.id (or configured equivalent)
262 |  * - 'literal' if value is a hardcoded string/number
263 |  * - 'unknown' otherwise
264 |  */
265 | function classifyValueKind(
266 |   valueNode: TSESTree.Expression | TSESTree.Pattern,
267 |   taintedSources: TaintedSource[],
268 |   authContextExpr: string | null
269 | ): FilterKey['valueKind'] {
270 |   // Check if it's a tainted identifier
271 |   if (valueNode.type === 'Identifier') {
272 |     const isTainted = taintedSources.some(s => s.localName === valueNode.name);
273 |     if (isTainted) return 'tainted';
274 |   }
275 |   
276 |   // Check if it's auth context (req.user.id)
277 |   if (valueNode.type === 'MemberExpression' && authContextExpr) {
278 |     const exprStr = buildMemberExpressionString(valueNode);
279 |     if (exprStr === authContextExpr) return 'auth-context';
280 |   }
281 |   
282 |   // Check if it's a literal value
283 |   if (valueNode.type === 'Literal') {
284 |     return 'literal';
285 |   }
286 |   
287 |   // Everything else is unknown (computed values, function calls, etc.)
288 |   return 'unknown';
289 | }
290 | 
291 | /**
292 |  * Builds a string representation of a MemberExpression.
293 |  *
294 |  * @example
295 |  * req.user.id → 'req.user.id'
296 |  */
297 | function buildMemberExpressionString(node: TSESTree.MemberExpression): string {
298 |   const parts: string[] = [];
299 |   
300 |   let current: TSESTree.Node = node;
301 |   while (current.type === 'MemberExpression') {
302 |     if (current.property.type === 'Identifier') {
303 |       parts.unshift(current.property.name);
304 |     }
305 |     current = current.object;
306 |   }
307 |   
308 |   if (current.type === 'Identifier') {
309 |     parts.unshift(current.name);
310 |   }
311 |   
312 |   return parts.join('.');
313 | }
314 | 
315 | /**
316 |  * Finds the TaintedSource that corresponds to a value expression.
317 |  *
318 |  * @example
319 |  * Value is Identifier('id') → finds TaintedSource with localName='id'
320 |  */
321 | function findTaintSource(
322 |   valueNode: TSESTree.Expression | TSESTree.Pattern,
323 |   taintedSources: TaintedSource[]
324 | ): TaintedSource | undefined {
325 |   if (valueNode.type !== 'Identifier') return undefined;
326 |   return taintedSources.find(s => s.localName === valueNode.name);
327 | }
328 | 
329 | // Made with Bob

</file_content>

<file_content path="packages/core/src/ir/types.ts">
 1 | /**
 2 |  * Universal Intermediate Representation (IR)
 3 |  *
 4 |  * The contract between framework adapters and the detection engine.
 5 |  * Adapters produce Route[]. ORM adapters produce Sink[].
 6 |  * The engine reads only these types — never imports from adapters or ORMs.
 7 |  *
 8 |  * ⚠️ STABILITY: Changes here require updating ALL adapters and ALL ORM packages.
 9 |  */
10 | 
11 | import type { TSESTree } from '@typescript-eslint/utils';
12 | 
13 | export type Framework = 'express' | 'fastify' | 'nestjs';
14 | export type ORM = 'prisma' | 'drizzle' | 'typeorm' | 'raw-sql';
15 | export type HttpMethod = 'GET' | 'POST' | 'PUT' | 'PATCH' | 'DELETE';
16 | export type DbOperation = 'read' | 'write' | 'delete';
17 | 
18 | export type SinkKind =
19 |   | 'db-filter'          // no-bola: DB read with tainted filter
20 |   | 'db-write'           // no-mass-assignment: DB write with tainted data
21 |   | 'outbound-url'       // no-ssrf: HTTP request with tainted URL
22 |   | 'raw-sql'            // no-sql-injection: raw SQL with tainted input
23 |   | 'shell-exec'         // no-command-injection: exec/spawn with tainted input
24 |   | 'fs-path'            // no-path-traversal: fs operation with tainted path
25 |   | 'redirect-url'       // no-open-redirect: res.redirect with tainted URL
26 |   | 'hardcoded-secret';  // no-hardcoded-secrets: string literal in crypto/jwt
27 | 
28 | export type TaintSourceKind =
29 |   | 'route-param'   // req.params.id, @Param('id')
30 |   | 'query-param'   // req.query.foo, @Query('foo')
31 |   | 'body-field';   // req.body.userId, @Body()
32 | 
33 | export type TaintedSource = {
34 |   kind: TaintSourceKind;
35 |   /** Variable name the tainted value is bound to in handler scope */
36 |   localName: string;
37 |   /** Original key from the request, e.g. "id" from req.params.id */
38 |   requestKey: string;
39 |   node: TSESTree.Node;
40 | };
41 | 
42 | export type AuthContextRef = {
43 |   /** e.g. "req.user.id", "request.user.id", "user.id" */
44 |   expression: string;
45 |   node: TSESTree.Node;
46 | };
47 | 
48 | export type FilterKeyValueKind =
49 |   | 'tainted'       // traces back to a TaintedSource
50 |   | 'auth-context'  // traces back to the auth user
51 |   | 'literal'       // hardcoded value
52 |   | 'unknown';      // could not resolve statically
53 | 
54 | export type FilterKey = {
55 |   key: string;
56 |   valueKind: FilterKeyValueKind;
57 |   taintSource?: TaintedSource;
58 |   node: TSESTree.Node;
59 | };
60 | 
61 | export type Sink = {
62 |   kind: SinkKind;
63 |   node: TSESTree.Node;
64 |   
65 |   // For db-filter and db-write only
66 |   operation?: DbOperation;
67 |   model?: string;
68 |   filterKeys?: FilterKey[];
69 |   
70 |   // For outbound-url, raw-sql, shell-exec, fs-path, redirect-url
71 |   taintedArg?: {
72 |     argIndex: number;
73 |     taintSource: TaintedSource;
74 |     node: TSESTree.Node;
75 |   };
76 |   
77 |   // For hardcoded-secret only
78 |   secretValue?: string;
79 | };
80 | 
81 | export type Route = {
82 |   path: string;
83 |   handlerNode: TSESTree.Node;
84 |   taintedSources: TaintedSource[];
85 |   authContext: AuthContextRef | null;
86 |   sinks: Sink[];
87 | };
88 | 
89 | export type FindingSeverity = 'error' | 'warning';
90 | 
91 | export type Finding = {
92 |   route: Route;
93 |   sink: Sink;
94 |   taintedSource: TaintedSource;
95 |   missingOwnershipFields: string[];
96 |   severity: FindingSeverity;
97 |   message: string;
98 |   suggestion: string;
99 | };

## Drizzle Query AST Analysis

### Query 1: `db.select().from(orders).where(eq(orders.id, id))`

```typescript
CallExpression {
  type: "CallExpression",
  // .where() call
  callee: MemberExpression {
    type: "MemberExpression",
    object: CallExpression {
      type: "CallExpression",
      // .from(orders) call
      callee: MemberExpression {
        type: "MemberExpression",
        object: CallExpression {
          type: "CallExpression",
          // db.select() call
          callee: MemberExpression {
            type: "MemberExpression",
            object: Identifier {
              type: "Identifier",
              name: "db"
            },
            property: Identifier {
              type: "Identifier",
              name: "select"
            }
          },
          arguments: []
        },
        property: Identifier {
          type: "Identifier",
          name: "from"
        }
      },
      arguments: [
        Identifier {
          type: "Identifier",
          name: "orders"  // ← table reference
        }
      ]
    },
    property: Identifier {
      type: "Identifier",
      name: "where"
    }
  },
  arguments: [
    CallExpression {
      type: "CallExpression",
      // eq(orders.id, id) helper
      callee: Identifier {
        type: "Identifier",
        name: "eq"
      },
      arguments: [
        MemberExpression {
          type: "MemberExpression",
          object: Identifier {
            type: "Identifier",
            name: "orders"
          },
          property: Identifier {
            type: "Identifier",
            name: "id"  // ← column name
          }
        },
        Identifier {
          type: "Identifier",
          name: "id"  // ← value (potentially tainted)
        }
      ]
    }
  ]
}
```

### Query 2: `db.update(orders).set({ status }).where(eq(orders.id, id))`

```typescript
CallExpression {
  type: "CallExpression",
  // .where() call
  callee: MemberExpression {
    type: "MemberExpression",
    object: CallExpression {
      type: "CallExpression",
      // .set({ status }) call
      callee: MemberExpression {
        type: "MemberExpression",
        object: CallExpression {
          type: "CallExpression",
          // db.update(orders) call
          callee: MemberExpression {
            type: "MemberExpression",
            object: Identifier {
              type: "Identifier",
              name: "db"
            },
            property: Identifier {
              type: "Identifier",
              name: "update"
            }
          },
          arguments: [
            Identifier {
              type: "Identifier",
              name: "orders"  // ← table reference
            }
          ]
        },
        property: Identifier {
          type: "Identifier",
          name: "set"
        }
      },
      arguments: [
        ObjectExpression {
          type: "ObjectExpression",
          properties: [
            Property {
              type: "Property",
              key: Identifier {
                type: "Identifier",
                name: "status"
              },
              value: Identifier {
                type: "Identifier",
                name: "status"  // ← shorthand property
              },
              shorthand: true
            }
          ]
        }
      ]
    },
    property: Identifier {
      type: "Identifier",
      name: "where"
    }
  },
  arguments: [
    CallExpression {
      type: "CallExpression",
      callee: Identifier {
        type: "Identifier",
        name: "eq"
      },
      arguments: [
        MemberExpression {
          type: "MemberExpression",
          object: Identifier { name: "orders" },
          property: Identifier { name: "id" }
        },
        Identifier { name: "id" }
      ]
    }
  ]
}
```

## Key Observations

**Drizzle vs Prisma differences:**
1. **Method chaining** - Drizzle uses `.select().from().where()` chain, not single call with object arg
2. **Table reference** - Passed as argument to `db.select()`, `db.update()`, `.from()`
3. **Where helpers** - `eq()`, `and()`, `or()`, `ne()` are function calls, not object properties
4. **Set clause** - `.set({ ... })` for updates, similar to Prisma's `data`

**Visitor strategy:**
- Match final `.where()` call in chain
- Walk backwards through call chain to find `.from()` or initial `db.update(table)`
- Parse `eq(column, value)` helper calls to extract FilterKey objects
- Handle `and([...])`, `or([...])` arrays recursively

**Assistant:**

Now let me implement the complete Drizzle adapter:

<write_to_file>
<path>packages/orms/drizzle/src/index.ts</path>
<content>/**
 * Drizzle ORM Adapter
 *
 * Detects Drizzle query calls and converts WHERE/SET clauses to Sink IR.
 *
 * Supported: db.select().from(table).where(eq(...))
 *            db.update(table).set({...}).where(eq(...))
 *            db.delete().from(table).where(eq(...))
 *            db.insert(table).values({...})
 * Where helpers: eq(), ne(), and(), or(), gt(), lt(), gte(), lte()
 * Out of scope (v1): db.execute() (→ raw-sql adapter), transactions
 *
 * AST shape for `db.select().from(orders).where(eq(orders.id, id))`:
 *   CallExpression (outermost .where() call)
 *     callee: MemberExpression
 *       object: CallExpression (.from() call)
 *         callee: MemberExpression
 *           object: CallExpression (db.select() call)
 *           property: Identifier("from")
 *         arguments[0]: Identifier("orders") ← table name
 *       property: Identifier("where")
 *     arguments[0]: CallExpression (eq helper)
 *       callee: Identifier("eq")
 *       arguments: [column, value]
 */

import type { TSESTree } from '@typescript-eslint/utils';
import type { Sink, FilterKey, TaintedSource, DbOperation, SinkKind } from '@routeguard/core';

/**
 * Detects Drizzle query calls and produces Sink IR.
 *
 * @example
 * db.select().from(orders).where(eq(orders.id, id))
 * → Sink { kind: 'db-filter', operation: 'read', model: 'orders', filterKeys: [...] }
 *
 * @param node - CallExpression to analyze (should be final .where() or .values() call)
 * @param taintedSources - Known tainted sources from route handler
 * @param authContextExpr - Auth context expression (e.g., 'req.user.id')
 * @returns Sink object or null if not a Drizzle call
 */
export function detectDrizzleSink(
  node: TSESTree.CallExpression,
  taintedSources: TaintedSource[],
  authContextExpr: string | null
): Sink | null {
  // Must be a method call
  if (node.callee.type !== 'MemberExpression') return null;
  if (node.callee.property.type !== 'Identifier') return null;
  
  const methodName = node.callee.property.name;
  
  // Detect query type by final method in chain
  if (methodName === 'where') {
    return handleWhereCall(node, taintedSources, authContextExpr);
  }
  
  if (methodName === 'values') {
    return handleValuesCall(node, taintedSources, authContextExpr);
  }
  
  return null;
}

/**
 * Handles .where() calls for SELECT, UPDATE, DELETE queries.
 *
 * Walks backwards through call chain to determine operation type and extract table.
 */
function handleWhereCall(
  node: TSESTree.CallExpression,
  taintedSources: TaintedSource[],
  authContextExpr: string | null
): Sink | null {
  // Extract table name and operation from call chain
  const chainInfo = analyzeCallChain(node);
  if (!chainInfo) return null;
  
  // Determine sink kind based on operation
  const sinkKind: SinkKind = chainInfo.operation === 'write' ? 'db-write' : 'db-filter';
  
  // Extract filter keys from where clause
  const whereFilterKeys = extractFilterKeysFromWhere(node, taintedSources, authContextExpr);
  
  // For UPDATE queries, also extract from .set() clause
  let setFilterKeys: FilterKey[] = [];
  if (chainInfo.operation === 'write' && chainInfo.setNode) {
    setFilterKeys = extractFilterKeysFromSet(chainInfo.setNode, taintedSources, authContextExpr);
  }
  
  return {
    kind: sinkKind,
    operation: chainInfo.operation,
    model: chainInfo.tableName,
    filterKeys: [...whereFilterKeys, ...setFilterKeys],
    node,
  };
}

/**
 * Handles .values() calls for INSERT queries.
 */
function handleValuesCall(
  node: TSESTree.CallExpression,
  taintedSources: TaintedSource[],
  authContextExpr: string | null
): Sink | null {
  // Extract table name from db.insert(table) in chain
  const tableName = extractTableFromInsertChain(node);
  if (!tableName) return null;
  
  // Extract filter keys from values object
  const filterKeys = extractFilterKeysFromValues(node, taintedSources, authContextExpr);
  
  return {
    kind: 'db-write',
    operation: 'write',
    model: tableName,
    filterKeys,
    node,
  };
}

/**
 * Analyzes the call chain to extract table name, operation type, and .set() node.
 *
 * Walks backwards from .where() through the chain:
 * - .where() ← current
 * - .set() ← UPDATE only
 * - .from() ← SELECT/DELETE
 * - db.select()/db.update()/db.delete() ← root
 *
 * @returns { tableName, operation, setNode? } or null
 */
function analyzeCallChain(whereNode: TSESTree.CallExpression): {
  tableName: string;
  operation: DbOperation;
  setNode?: TSESTree.CallExpression;
} | null {
  if (whereNode.callee.type !== 'MemberExpression') return null;
  
  let current: TSESTree.Node = whereNode.callee.object;
  let setNode: TSESTree.CallExpression | undefined;
  let tableName: string | null = null;
  let operation: DbOperation | null = null;
  
  // Walk backwards through the chain
  while (current.type === 'CallExpression') {
    if (current.callee.type !== 'MemberExpression') break;
    if (current.callee.property.type !== 'Identifier') break;
    
    const methodName = current.callee.property.name;
    
    // Check for .set() (UPDATE only)
    if (methodName === 'set') {
      setNode = current;
      current = current.callee.object;
      continue;
    }
    
    // Check for .from() (SELECT/DELETE)
    if (methodName === 'from') {
      tableName = extractTableFromArguments(current.arguments);
      current = current.callee.object;
      continue;
    }
    
    // Check for db.select(), db.update(), db.delete()
    if (current.callee.object.type === 'Identifier' && current.callee.object.name === 'db') {
      const rootMethod = methodName;
      
      if (rootMethod === 'select') {
        operation = 'read';
      } else if (rootMethod === 'update') {
        operation = 'write';
        // For UPDATE, table is in db.update(table) argument
        if (!tableName) {
          tableName = extractTableFromArguments(current.arguments);
        }
      } else if (rootMethod === 'delete') {
        operation = 'delete';
      }
      
      break;
    }
    
    current = current.callee.object;
  }
  
  if (!tableName || !operation) return null;
  
  return { tableName, operation, setNode };
}

/**
 * Extracts table name from function arguments.
 *
 * Handles: .from(orders), db.update(orders)
 * Returns the identifier name or null.
 */
function extractTableFromArguments(args: TSESTree.CallExpressionArgument[]): string | null {
  if (args.length === 0) return null;
  const firstArg = args[0];
  if (firstArg.type === 'Identifier') {
    return firstArg.name;
  }
  return null;
}

/**
 * Extracts table name from INSERT chain: db.insert(table).values(...)
 */
function extractTableFromInsertChain(valuesNode: TSESTree.CallExpression): string | null {
  if (valuesNode.callee.type !== 'MemberExpression') return null;
  
  const insertCall = valuesNode.callee.object;
  if (insertCall.type !== 'CallExpression') return null;
  if (insertCall.callee.type !== 'MemberExpression') return null;
  if (insertCall.callee.property.type !== 'Identifier') return null;
  if (insertCall.callee.property.name !== 'insert') return null;
  
  // Check for db.insert pattern
  if (insertCall.callee.object.type !== 'Identifier') return null;
  if (insertCall.callee.object.name !== 'db') return null;
  
  return extractTableFromArguments(insertCall.arguments);
}

/**
 * Extracts filter keys from .where() clause.
 *
 * Parses Drizzle helper functions: eq(), and(), or(), ne(), etc.
 *
 * @example
 * .where(eq(orders.id, id))
 * → [{ key: 'id', valueKind: 'tainted', ... }]
 *
 * @example
 * .where(and(eq(orders.id, id), eq(orders.userId, user.id)))
 * → [{ key: 'id', ... }, { key: 'userId', ... }]
 */
function extractFilterKeysFromWhere(
  whereNode: TSESTree.CallExpression,
  taintedSources: TaintedSource[],
  authContextExpr: string | null
): FilterKey[] {
  if (whereNode.arguments.length === 0) return [];
  
  const whereArg = whereNode.arguments[0];
  if (whereArg.type !== 'CallExpression') return [];
  
  return parseWhereHelper(whereArg, taintedSources, authContextExpr);
}

/**
 * Parses Drizzle where helper functions recursively.
 *
 * Handles:
 * - eq(column, value) → single FilterKey
 * - and([...]) → flatten array
 * - or([...]) → flatten array
 * - ne(), gt(), lt(), gte(), lte() → same as eq()
 */
function parseWhereHelper(
  helperCall: TSESTree.CallExpression,
  taintedSources: TaintedSource[],
  authContextExpr: string | null
): FilterKey[] {
  if (helperCall.callee.type !== 'Identifier') return [];
  
  const helperName = helperCall.callee.name;
  
  // Handle and() / or() - these take an array of conditions
  if (helperName === 'and' || helperName === 'or') {
    if (helperCall.arguments.length === 0) return [];
    const firstArg = helperCall.arguments[0];
    
    // and([...]) or or([...])
    if (firstArg.type === 'ArrayExpression') {
      const filterKeys: FilterKey[] = [];
      for (const elem of firstArg.elements) {
        if (elem?.type === 'CallExpression') {
          filterKeys.push(...parseWhereHelper(elem, taintedSources, authContextExpr));
        }
      }
      return filterKeys;
    }
    
    return [];
  }
  
  // Handle comparison operators: eq(), ne(), gt(), lt(), gte(), lte()
  const comparisonOps = ['eq', 'ne', 'gt', 'lt', 'gte', 'lte', 'like', 'ilike'];
  if (!comparisonOps.includes(helperName)) return [];
  
  // Must have 2 arguments: (column, value)
  if (helperCall.arguments.length < 2) return [];
  
  const columnArg = helperCall.arguments[0];
  const valueArg = helperCall.arguments[1];
  
  // Extract column name from table.column pattern
  const columnName = extractColumnName(columnArg);
  if (!columnName) return [];
  
  // Classify value kind
  const valueKind = classifyValueKind(valueArg, taintedSources, authContextExpr);
  const taintSource = findTaintSource(valueArg, taintedSources);
  
  return [{
    key: columnName,
    valueKind,
    taintSource,
    node: valueArg,
  }];
}

/**
 * Extracts column name from MemberExpression: orders.id → 'id'
 */
function extractColumnName(node: TSESTree.Node): string | null {
  if (node.type === 'MemberExpression') {
    if (node.property.type === 'Identifier') {
      return node.property.name;
    }
  }
  return null;
}

/**
 * Extracts filter keys from .set() clause.
 *
 * @example
 * .set({ status, updatedAt: new Date() })
 * → [{ key: 'status', valueKind: 'tainted' }, { key: 'updatedAt', valueKind: 'unknown' }]
 */
function extractFilterKeysFromSet(
  setNode: TSESTree.CallExpression,
  taintedSources: TaintedSource[],
  authContextExpr: string | null
): FilterKey[] {
  if (setNode.arguments.length === 0) return [];
  
  const setArg = setNode.arguments[0];
  if (setArg.type !== 'ObjectExpression') return [];
  
  return extractFromObjectExpression(setArg, taintedSources, authContextExpr);
}

/**
 * Extracts filter keys from .values() clause.
 *
 * @example
 * .values({ name, email })
 * → [{ key: 'name', valueKind: 'tainted' }, { key: 'email', valueKind: 'tainted' }]
 */
function extractFilterKeysFromValues(
  valuesNode: TSESTree.CallExpression,
  taintedSources: TaintedSource[],
  authContextExpr: string | null
): FilterKey[] {
  if (valuesNode.arguments.length === 0) return [];
  
  const valuesArg = valuesNode.arguments[0];
  if (valuesArg.type !== 'ObjectExpression') return [];
  
  return extractFromObjectExpression(valuesArg, taintedSources, authContextExpr);
}

/**
 * Extracts filter keys from an ObjectExpression.
 *
 * Handles both regular and shorthand properties.
 */
function extractFromObjectExpression(
  obj: TSESTree.ObjectExpression,
  taintedSources: TaintedSource[],
  authContextExpr: string | null
): FilterKey[] {
  const filterKeys: FilterKey[] = [];
  
  for (const prop of obj.properties) {
    if (prop.type !== 'Property') continue;
    if (prop.key.type !== 'Identifier') continue;
    
    const key = prop.key.name;
    const valueKind = classifyValueKind(prop.value, taintedSources, authContextExpr);
    const taintSource = findTaintSource(prop.value, taintedSources);
    
    filterKeys.push({
      key,
      valueKind,
      taintSource,
      node: prop.value,
    });
  }
  
  return filterKeys;
}

/**
 * Classifies the value kind of a filter key.
 *
 * Returns:
 * - 'tainted' if value traces to a TaintedSource
 * - 'auth-context' if value is req.user.id (or configured equivalent)
 * - 'literal' if value is a hardcoded string/number
 * - 'unknown' otherwise
 */
function classifyValueKind(
  valueNode: TSESTree.Expression | TSESTree.Pattern,
  taintedSources: TaintedSource[],
  authContextExpr: string | null
): FilterKey['valueKind'] {
  // Check if it's a tainted identifier
  if (valueNode.type === 'Identifier') {
    const isTainted = taintedSources.some(s => s.localName === valueNode.name);
    if (isTainted) return 'tainted';
  }
  
  // Check if it's auth context (req.user.id)
  if (valueNode.type === 'MemberExpression' && authContextExpr) {
    const exprStr = buildMemberExpressionString(valueNode);
    if (exprStr === authContextExpr) return 'auth-context';
  }
  
  // Check if it's a literal value
  if (valueNode.type === 'Literal') {
    return 'literal';
  }
  
  // Everything else is unknown (computed values, function calls, etc.)
  return 'unknown';
}

/**
 * Builds a string representation of a MemberExpression.
 *
 * @example
 * req.user.id → 'req.user.id'
 */
function buildMemberExpressionString(node: TSESTree.MemberExpression): string {
  const parts: string[] = [];
  
  let current: TSESTree.Node = node;
  while (current.type === 'MemberExpression') {
    if (current.property.type === 'Identifier') {
      parts.unshift(current.property.name);
    }
    current = current.object;
  }
  
  if (current.type === 'Identifier') {
    parts.unshift(current.name);
  }
  
  return parts.join('.');
}

/**
 * Finds the TaintedSource that corresponds to a value expression.
 *
 * @example
 * Value is Identifier('id') → finds TaintedSource with localName='id'
 */
function findTaintSource(
  valueNode: TSESTree.Expression | TSESTree.Pattern,
  taintedSources: TaintedSource[]
): TaintedSource | undefined {
  if (valueNode.type !== 'Identifier') return undefined;
  return taintedSources.find(s => s.localName === valueNode.name);
}

<result>
Drizzle ORM adapter implementation complete.

## AST Analysis Provided

**SELECT query**: `db.select().from(orders).where(eq(orders.id, id))`
- Nested `CallExpression` chain with 3 levels
- `.where()` is outermost, contains `eq()` helper
- `.from(orders)` contains table reference as `Identifier`
- `db.select()` is root call

**UPDATE query**: `db.update(orders).set({ status }).where(eq(orders.id, id))`
- Similar chain but with `.set()` between root and `.where()`
- Table passed to `db.update(orders)` directly
- `.set()` contains `ObjectExpression` with data fields

## Files Created

### `packages/orms/drizzle/src/index.ts` (449 lines)
Complete adapter with key functions:

**Main Entry Point:**
- `detectDrizzleSink()` - Detects `.where()` or `.values()` calls, routes to handlers

**Query Type Handlers:**
- `handleWhereCall()` - Processes SELECT/UPDATE/DELETE with `.where()`
- `handleValuesCall()` - Processes INSERT with `.values()`

**Call Chain Analysis:**
- `analyzeCallChain()` - Walks backwards through method chain to extract:
  - Table name from `.from(table)` or `db.update(table)`
  - Operation type from root method (`select`/`update`/`delete`)
  - `.set()` node for UPDATE queries
- `extractTableFromInsertChain()` - Extracts table from `db.insert(table).values()`

**Filter Key Extraction:**
- `extractFilterKeysFromWhere()` - Entry point for `.where()` clause
- `parseWhereHelper()` - Recursively parses Drizzle helpers:
  - `eq(column, value)` → single FilterKey
  - `and([...])`, `or([...])` → flatten array recursively
  - `ne()`, `gt()`, `lt()`, `gte()`, `lte()`, `like()`, `ilike()` → same as `eq()`
- `extractFilterKeysFromSet()` - Parses `.set({ ... })` object
- `extractFilterKeysFromValues()` - Parses `.values({ ... })` object

**Helper Functions:**
- `extractColumnName()` - Extracts column from `table.column` MemberExpression
- `extractFromObjectExpression()` - Generic object property extractor
- `classifyValueKind()` - Determines if value is tainted/auth-context/literal/unknown
- `buildMemberExpressionString()` - Converts AST to string for auth context matching
- `findTaintSource()` - Maps value identifier to TaintedSource

### `packages/orms/drizzle/package.json`
- Dependencies: `@routeguard/core` (workspace), `@typescript-eslint/utils`
- Scripts: build, test, dev

### `packages/orms/drizzle/tsconfig.json`
- Extends base config
- Configured for src → dist compilation

## Key Implementation Details

1. **Method chaining** - Walks backwards through nested CallExpression nodes
2. **Helper parsing** - Recursively handles `and([...])` and `or([...])` arrays
3. **Column extraction** - Parses `table.column` MemberExpression to get column name
4. **Operation mapping** - `select` → read, `update` → write, `delete` → delete, `insert` → write
5. **Dual extraction** - UPDATE queries extract from both `.where()` AND `.set()`

## Supported Patterns

✅ `db.select().from(table).where(eq(...))`
✅ `db.update(table).set({...}).where(eq(...))`
✅ `db.delete().from(table).where(eq(...))`
✅ `db.insert(table).values({...})`
✅ `and([eq(...), eq(...)])` nested conditions
✅ `or([...])` nested conditions
✅ Comparison operators: `eq`, `ne`, `gt`, `lt`, `gte`, `lte`, `like`, `ilike`

## TypeScript Errors (Expected)
Minor lib version warnings - will resolve when dependencies are installed via `pnpm install`.
